<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="H.EC.A1.B0">H조</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2002%EB%85%84_FIFA_%EC%9B%94%EB%93%9C%EC%BB%B5_%EC%84%A0%EC%88%98_%EB%AA%85%EB%8B%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="부분 편집: H조">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
